# Get Accounts

```ts
async getAccounts(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Accounts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Accounts array with 0 to n Account

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status==&quot;ACTIVE&quot; AND Type==&quot;BANK&quot;';

const order = 'Name ASC';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getAccounts(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Accounts": [
    {
      "AccountID": "ebd06280-af70-4bed-97c6-7451a454ad85",
      "Code": "091",
      "Name": "Business Savings Account",
      "Type": "BANK",
      "TaxType": "NONE",
      "EnablePaymentsToAccount": false,
      "BankAccountNumber": "0209087654321050",
      "BankAccountType": "BANK",
      "CurrencyCode": "NZD"
    },
    {
      "AccountID": "7d05a53d-613d-4eb2-a2fc-dcb6adb80b80",
      "Code": "200",
      "Name": "Sales",
      "Type": "REVENUE",
      "TaxType": "OUTPUT2",
      "Description": "Income from any normal business activity",
      "EnablePaymentsToAccount": false
    }
  ]
}
```


# Create Account

```ts
async createAccount(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Account,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Accounts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Account`](../../doc/models/account.md) | Body, Required | Account object in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - created new Account and return response of type Accounts array with new Account

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: Account = {
  code: '123456',
  description: 'Hello World',
  name: 'Foobar',
  type: AccountTypeEnum.EXPENSE,
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createAccount(
    xeroTenantId,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "11814c9d-3b5e-492e-93b0-fad16bf3244f",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
```

# Delete Account

```ts
async deleteAccount(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  accountID: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Accounts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `accountID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for retrieving single object |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - delete existing Account and return response of type Accounts array with deleted Account

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const accountID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

  const response = await accountingController.deleteAccount(
    xeroTenantId,
    accountID
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Update Account

```ts
async updateAccount(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  accountID: string,
  body: Accounts,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Accounts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `accountID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for retrieving single object |
| `body` | [`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md) | Body, Required | Request of type Accounts array with one Account |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - update existing Account and return response of type Accounts array with updated Account

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const accountID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: Accounts = {
  accounts: [
    {
      accountID: '99ce6032-0678-4aa0-8148-240c75fee33a',
      code: '123456',
      description: 'GoodBye World',
      enablePaymentsToAccount: false,
      name: 'BarFoo',
      reportingCode: 'EXP',
      showInExpenseClaims: false,
      taxType: 'INPUT',
      type: AccountTypeEnum.EXPENSE,
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateAccount(
    xeroTenantId,
    accountID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

```json
    {
      "AccountID": "99ce6032-0678-4aa0-8148-240c75fee33a",

      "Name": "BarFoo",
```

`accounting.attachments.read`

# Update Account Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateAccountAttachmentByFileName(
```

| `accountID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Account object |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the attachment |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

`accounting.attachments`

```ts
    xeroTenantId,
    accountID,

  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
```

# Get Bank Transactions

```ts
async getBankTransactions(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  page?: number,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<BankTransactions>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Up to 100 bank transactions will be returned in a single API call with line items details |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BankTransactions array with 0 to n BankTransaction

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

const order = 'Type ASC';

const page = 1;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getBankTransactions(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    page,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
```

# Update or Create Bank Transactions

```ts
async updateOrCreateBankTransactions(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: BankTransactions,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<BankTransactions>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BankTransactions array with new BankTransaction

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: BankTransactions = {
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreateBankTransactions(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Create Bank Transactions

```ts
async createBankTransactions(
```

# Get Bank Transaction

```ts
async getBankTransaction(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  bankTransactionID: string,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<BankTransactions>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

```ts
    unitdp

  console.log(response.statusCode);
```

# Get Bank Transaction Attachments

```ts
async getBankTransactionAttachments(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  bankTransactionID: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with 0 to n Attachment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const bankTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getBankTransactionAttachments(
    xeroTenantId,
    bankTransactionID
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "c50798e1-29e9-4a30-a452-bb6e42e400c8",
  "Status": "OK",

      "ContentLength": 2878711
    },
    {
```

# Get Bank Transaction Attachment by Id

```ts
async getBankTransactionAttachmentById(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  bankTransactionID: string,
  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for an attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for BankTransaction as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const bankTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const contentType = 'image/jpg';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getBankTransactionAttachmentById(
    xeroTenantId,
    bankTransactionID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update Bank Transaction Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateBankTransactionAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  bankTransactionID: string,
  fileName: string,
  body: FileWrapper,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of Attachments array of Attachment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const bankTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

const body = new FileWrapper(fs.createReadStream('dummy_file'));

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateBankTransactionAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    bankTransactionID,
    fileName,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json

  "Id": "572ad2fe-8c23-45aa-82f9-864485327685",
  "Status": "OK",

  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "4508a692-e52c-4ad8-a138-2f13e22bf57b",
      "FileName": "sample5.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/BankTransactions/db54aab0-ad40-4ced-bcff-0940ba20db2c/Attachments/sample5.jpg",
```

# Get Bank Transfers

```ts
async getBankTransfers(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<BankTransfers>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of BankTransfers array of 0 to N BankTransfer

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`BankTransfers`](../../doc/models/bank-transfers.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'HasAttachments==true';

const order = 'Amount ASC';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getBankTransfers(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "dfc0d130-9007-4a98-a5ef-6f01700f18e2",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1551311318988)/",
  "BankTransfers": [
    {
      "BankTransferID": "6221458a-ef7a-4d5f-9b1c-1b96ce03833c",
      "CreatedDateUTCString": "2016-10-17T20:46:01",
      "CreatedDateUTC": "/Date(1476737161140+0000)/",
```

# Create Bank Transfer

```ts
async createBankTransfer(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: BankTransfers,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<BankTransfers>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`BankTransfers`](../../doc/models/bank-transfers.md) | Body, Required | BankTransfers with array of BankTransfer objects in request body |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of BankTransfers array of one BankTransfer

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`BankTransfers`](../../doc/models/bank-transfers.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: BankTransfers = {
  bankTransfers: [
    {
      amount: 50,
      fromBankAccount: {
        accountID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
        bankAccountNumber: '123455',
        bankAccountType: BankAccountTypeEnum.BANK,
        code: '090',
        currencyCode: CurrencyCodeEnum.USD,
        enablePaymentsToAccount: false,
        name: 'My Savings',
        reportingCode: 'ASS',
        showInExpenseClaims: false,
        status: StatusEnum.ACTIVE,
        taxType: 'NONE',
        type: AccountTypeEnum.BANK,
      },
      toBankAccount: {
        accountID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
        bankAccountNumber: '123455',
        bankAccountType: BankAccountTypeEnum.BANK,
        code: '088',
        currencyCode: CurrencyCodeEnum.USD,
        enablePaymentsToAccount: false,
        name: 'Business Wells Fargo',
        reportingCode: 'ASS',
        showInExpenseClaims: false,
        status: StatusEnum.ACTIVE,
        taxType: 'NONE',
        type: AccountTypeEnum.BANK,
      },
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createBankTransfer(
    xeroTenantId,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "ae767b68-affd-4e17-bac0-83eaf1854dcd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1551311317475)/",
  "BankTransfers": [
    {
      "BankTransferID": "76eea4b6-f026-464c-b6f3-5fb39a196145",
      "DateString": "2019-02-27T00:00:00",
      "Date": "/Date(1551225600000+0000)/",
      "FromBankAccount": {
        "AccountID": "7e5e243b-9fcd-4aef-8e3a-c70be1e39bfa",
        "Code": "090",
        "Name": "My Savings"
      },
      "ToBankAccount": {
        "AccountID": "6f7594f2-f059-4d56-9e67-47ac9733bfe9",
        "Code": "088",
        "Name": "Business Wells Fargo"
      },
      "Amount": 50.0,
      "FromBankTransactionID": "e4059952-5acb-4a56-b076-53fad85f2930",
      "ToBankTransactionID": "88e4ac17-293b-4e5a-8d8b-3ce3a0b1ee17",
      "CurrencyRate": 1.0,
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |

# Get Bank Transfer Attachment by Id

```ts
async getBankTransferAttachmentById(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  bankTransferID: string,
  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransferID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transfer |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for an Attachment to a bank transfer |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of binary data from the Attachment to a Bank Transfer

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const bankTransferID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const contentType = 'image/jpg';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getBankTransferAttachmentById(
    xeroTenantId,
    bankTransferID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update Bank Transfer Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateBankTransferAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  bankTransferID: string,
  fileName: string,
  body: FileWrapper,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransferID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transfer |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached to a Bank Transfer |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of Attachments array of 0 to N Attachment for a Bank Transfer

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const bankTransferID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

const body = new FileWrapper(fs.createReadStream('dummy_file'));

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateBankTransferAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    bankTransferID,
    fileName,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json

  "Id": "c7810140-19c2-4ff7-b3ec-b7e95ce7becf",

  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "0851935c-c4c5-4de8-9247-ce22efde6f82",

      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/BankTransfers/6221458a-ef7a-4d5f-9b1c-1b96ce03833c/Attachments/sample5.jpg",
```

# Create Bank Transfer History Record

```ts
async createBankTransferHistoryRecord(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  bankTransferID: string,
  body: HistoryRecords,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<HistoryRecords>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransferID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transfer |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const bankTransferID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: HistoryRecords = {
  historyRecords: [
    {
      details: 'Hello World',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createBankTransferHistoryRecord(
    xeroTenantId,
    bankTransferID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Batch Payments

Batch payments allow you to bundle multiple bills or invoices into one payment transaction. This means a single payment in Xero can be reconciled with a single transaction on the bank statement making for a much simpler bank reconciliation experience.

```ts
async getBatchPayments(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<BatchPayments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BatchPayments array of BatchPayment objects

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`BatchPayments`](../../doc/models/batch-payments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

const order = 'Date ASC';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getBatchPayments(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Create Batch Payment

Batch payments allow you to bundle multiple bills or invoices into one payment transaction. This means a single payment in Xero can be reconciled with a single transaction on the bank statement making for a much simpler bank reconciliation experience.

```ts
async createBatchPayment(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: BatchPayments,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<BatchPayments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`BatchPayments`](../../doc/models/batch-payments.md) | Body, Required | BatchPayments with an array of Payments in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BatchPayments array of BatchPayment objects

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`BatchPayments`](../../doc/models/batch-payments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: BatchPayments = {
  batchPayments: [
    {
      account: {
        accountID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      },
      date: '2018-08-01',
      payments: [
        {
          account: {
            code: '001',
          },
          amount: 500,
          date: '2019-12-31',
          invoice: {
            contact: {
            },
            invoiceID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
            lineItems: [],
            type: Type3Enum.ACCPAY,
          },
        }
      ],
      reference: 'ref',
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createBatchPayment(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Branding Theme Payment Services

```ts
async getBrandingThemePaymentServices(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  brandingThemeID: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<PaymentServices>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `brandingThemeID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Branding Theme |

# Get Contacts

```ts
async getContacts(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  iDs?: string[],
  page?: number,
  includeArchived?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Contacts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `iDs` | `string[] \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma separated list of ContactIDs. Allows you to retrieve a specific set of contacts in a single call. |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 - Up to 100 contacts will be returned in a single API call. |
| `includeArchived` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. includeArchived=true - Contacts with a status of ARCHIVED will be included in the response |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Contacts array with 0 to N Contact

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'ContactStatus==&quot;ACTIVE&quot;';

const order = 'Name ASC';

const page = 1;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getContacts(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    undefined,
    page
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update or Create Contacts

```ts
async updateOrCreateContacts(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Contacts,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Contacts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Contacts array with newly created Contact

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: Contacts = {
  contacts: [
    {
      emailAddress: 'hulk@avengers.com',
      name: 'Bruce Banner',
      paymentTerms: {
        bills: {
          day: 15,
          type: PaymentTermTypeEnum.OFCURRENTMONTH,
        },
        sales: {
          day: 10,
          type: PaymentTermTypeEnum.DAYSAFTERBILLMONTH,
        },
      },
      phones: [
        {
          phoneAreaCode: '415',
          phoneNumber: '555-1212',
          phoneType: PhoneTypeEnum.MOBILE,
        }
      ],
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreateContacts(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "e997d6d7-6dad-4458-beb8-d9c1bf7f2edf",
```

# Create Contacts

```ts
async createContacts(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Contacts,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Contacts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md) | Body, Required | Contacts with an array of Contact objects to create in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Contacts array with newly created Contact

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

          day: 10,

        {
          phoneAreaCode: '',
          phoneCountryCode: '',

        },

          phoneAreaCode: '',

      purchasesTrackingCategories: [],
      salesTrackingCategories: [],
    }
  ],
};

    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
```

# Update Contact

```ts
async updateContact(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  contactID: string,
  body: Contacts,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Contacts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `body` | [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md) | Body, Required | an array of Contacts containing single Contact object with properties to update |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Contacts array with an updated Contact

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

  contacts: [
    {
      contactID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      name: 'Thanos',
    }
  ],
};

    xeroTenantId,
    contactID,
    body
  );

  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.

    // Extracting response error headers.
```

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

```ts
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);

}
```

# Get Contact Attachment by Id

```ts
async getContactAttachmentById(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  contactID: string,
  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Contact as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const contentType = 'image/jpg';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getContactAttachmentById(
    xeroTenantId,
    contactID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update Contact Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateContactAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  contactID: string,
  fileName: string,
  body: FileWrapper,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name for the file you are attaching |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with an updated Attachment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

const body = new FileWrapper(fs.createReadStream('dummy_file'));

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateContactAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    contactID,
    fileName,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Credit Notes

```ts
async getCreditNotes(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  page?: number,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<CreditNotes>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 credit notes will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each credit note |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Credit Notes array of CreditNote

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="DRAFT"';

const order = 'CreditNoteNumber ASC';

const page = 1;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getCreditNotes(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    page,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

# Update or Create Credit Notes

```ts
async updateOrCreateCreditNotes(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: CreditNotes,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<CreditNotes>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md) | Body, Required | an array of Credit Notes with a single CreditNote object. |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Credit Notes array of newly created CreditNote

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: CreditNotes = {
  creditNotes: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8',
      },
      date: '2019-01-05',
      lineItems: [
        {
          accountCode: '400',
          description: 'Foobar',
          quantity: 2,
          unitAmount: 20,
        }
      ],
      reference: 'HelloWorld',
      status: Status7Enum.AUTHORISED,
      type: Type4Enum.ACCPAYCREDIT,
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreateCreditNotes(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Create Credit Notes

```ts
async createCreditNotes(
```

| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

# Get Credit Note

```ts
async getCreditNote(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  creditNoteID: string,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<CreditNotes>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Credit Notes array with a unique CreditNote

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const unitdp = 4;

  const response = await accountingController.getCreditNote(
    xeroTenantId,
    creditNoteID,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.

  if (error instanceof ApiError) {

    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update Credit Note

```ts
async updateCreditNote(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  creditNoteID: string,
  body: CreditNotes,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<CreditNotes>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `body` | [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md) | Body, Required | an array of Credit Notes containing credit note details to update |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Credit Notes array with updated CreditNote

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: CreditNotes = {
  creditNotes: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8',
      },
      date: '2019-01-05',
      lineItems: [
        {
          accountCode: '400',
          description: 'Foobar',
          quantity: 2,
          unitAmount: 20,
        }
      ],
      reference: 'HelloWorld',
      status: Status7Enum.AUTHORISED,
      type: Type4Enum.ACCPAYCREDIT,
    }
  ],
};

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateCreditNote(
    xeroTenantId,
    creditNoteID,
    body,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Create Credit Note Allocation

```ts
async createCreditNoteAllocation(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  creditNoteID: string,
  body: Allocations,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Allocations>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `body` | [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md) | Body, Required | Allocations with array of Allocation object in body of request. |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Allocations array with newly created Allocation for specific Credit Note

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: Allocations = {
  allocations: [
    {
      amount: 1,
      date: '2019-03-05',
      invoice: {
        invoiceID: 'c45720a1-ade3-4a38-a064-d15489be6841',
        lineItems: [],
      },
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createCreditNoteAllocation(
    xeroTenantId,
    creditNoteID,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Credit Note Attachment by Id

```ts
async getCreditNoteAttachmentById(
```

| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

```ts
    xeroTenantId,
    creditNoteID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.

  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`

  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.

    // Extracting response error headers.

    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
```

# Update Credit Note Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateCreditNoteAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  creditNoteID: string,

  body: FileWrapper,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
```

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |

| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the file you are attaching to Credit Note |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

```ts
    xeroTenantId,

    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.

      console.log(error.result);
```

## Example Usage

```ts
  const response = await accountingController.getCreditNoteHistory(
    xeroTenantId,
    creditNoteID
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Create Credit Note History

```ts
async createCreditNoteHistory(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  creditNoteID: string,
  body: HistoryRecords,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<HistoryRecords>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: HistoryRecords = {
  historyRecords: [
    {
      details: 'Hello World',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createCreditNoteHistory(
    xeroTenantId,
    creditNoteID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

```ts
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {

    // Extracting response error headers.
```

# Update or Create Employees

```ts
async updateOrCreateEmployees(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Employees,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Employees>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Employees`](../../doc/models/employees.md) | Body, Required | Employees with array of Employee object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Employees array with new Employee

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Employees`](../../doc/models/employees.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const body: Employees = {
  employees: [
    {
      externalLink: {
        url: 'http://twitter.com/#!/search/Nick+Fury',
      },
      firstName: 'Nick',
      lastName: 'Fury',
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreateEmployees(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Create Expense Claims

```ts
async createExpenseClaims(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: ExpenseClaims,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ExpenseClaims>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md) | Body, Required | ExpenseClaims with array of ExpenseClaim object in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ExpenseClaims array with newly created ExpenseClaim

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: ExpenseClaims = {
  expenseClaims: [
    {
      receipts: [
        {
          receiptID: 'dc1c7f6d-0a4c-402f-acac-551d62ce5816',
        }
      ],
      status: Status12Enum.SUBMITTED,
      user: {
        userID: 'd1164823-0ac1-41ad-987b-b4e30fe0b273',
      },
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createExpenseClaims(
    xeroTenantId,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```
