# Update Expense Claim

```ts
async updateExpenseClaim(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  expenseClaimID: string,
  body: ExpenseClaims,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ExpenseClaims>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `expenseClaimID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a ExpenseClaim |
| `body` | [`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ExpenseClaims array with updated ExpenseClaim

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const expenseClaimID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: ExpenseClaims = {
  expenseClaims: [
    {
      receipts: [
        {
          receiptID: 'dc1c7f6d-0a4c-402f-acac-551d62ce5816',
        }
      ],
      status: Status12Enum.SUBMITTED,
      user: {
        userID: 'd1164823-0ac1-41ad-987b-b4e30fe0b273',
      },
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateExpenseClaim(
    xeroTenantId,
    expenseClaimID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Invoices

```ts
async getInvoices(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  iDs?: string[],
  invoiceNumbers?: string[],
  contactIDs?: string[],
  statuses?: string[],
  page?: number,
  includeArchived?: boolean,
  createdByMyApp?: boolean,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Invoices>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `iDs` | `string[] \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma-separated list of InvoicesIDs. |
| `invoiceNumbers` | `string[] \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma-separated list of InvoiceNumbers. |
| `contactIDs` | `string[] \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma-separated list of ContactIDs. |
| `statuses` | `string[] \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma-separated list Statuses. For faster response times we recommend using these explicit parameters instead of passing OR conditions into the Where filter. |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 invoices will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each invoice |
| `includeArchived` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. includeArchived=true - Contacts with a status of ARCHIVED will be included in the response |
| `createdByMyApp` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | When set to true you'll only retrieve Invoices created by your app |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with all Invoices

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="DRAFT"';

const order = 'InvoiceNumber ASC';

const page = 1;

const createdByMyApp = false;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getInvoices(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    undefined,
    undefined,
    undefined,
    undefined,
    page,
    undefined,
    createdByMyApp,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update or Create Invoices

```ts
async updateOrCreateInvoices(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Invoices,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Invoices>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with newly created Invoice

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: Invoices = {
  invoices: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8',
      },
      date: '2019-03-11',
      dueDate: '2018-12-10',
      lineItems: [
        {
          accountCode: '200',
          description: 'Acme Tires',
          lineAmount: 40,
          quantity: 2,
          taxType: 'NONE',
          unitAmount: 20,
        }
      ],
      reference: 'Website Design',
      status: Status5Enum.AUTHORISED,
      type: Type3Enum.ACCREC,
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreateInvoices(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Create Invoices

```ts
async createInvoices(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Invoices,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Invoices>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md) | Body, Required | Invoices with an array of invoice objects in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with newly created Invoice

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const body: Invoices = {
  invoices: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8',
      },
      date: '2019-03-11',
      dueDate: '2018-12-10',
      lineItems: [
        {
          accountCode: '200',
          description: 'Acme Tires',
          lineAmount: 40,
          quantity: 2,
          taxType: 'NONE',
          unitAmount: 20,
        }
      ],
      reference: 'Website Design',
      status: Status5Enum.AUTHORISED,
      type: Type3Enum.ACCREC,
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createInvoices(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Invoice

```ts
async getInvoice(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  invoiceID: string,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Invoices>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with specified Invoices

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getInvoice(
    xeroTenantId,
    invoiceID,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update Invoice

```ts
async updateInvoice(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  invoiceID: string,
  body: Invoices,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Invoices>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `body` | [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with updated Invoice

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: Invoices = {
  invoices: [
    {
      contact: {
      },
      invoiceID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      lineItems: [],
      reference: 'May the force be with you',
      type: Type3Enum.ACCPAY,
    }
  ],
};

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateInvoice(
    xeroTenantId,
    invoiceID,
    body,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Invoice Attachments

```ts
async getInvoiceAttachments(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  invoiceID: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array of Attachments for specified Invoices

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
    invoiceID
  );

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Get Invoice Attachment by Id

```ts
async getInvoiceAttachmentById(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  invoiceID: string,
  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Invoice as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const contentType = 'image/jpg';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getInvoiceAttachmentById(
    xeroTenantId,
    invoiceID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update Invoice Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  invoiceID: string,
  fileName: string,
  body: FileWrapper,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the file you are attaching |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with updated Attachment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    invoiceID,
    fileName,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Create Invoice Attachment by File Name

```ts
async createInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  invoiceID: string,
  fileName: string,
  body: FileWrapper,
  includeOnline?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the file you are attaching |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `includeOnline` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Allows an attachment to be seen by the end customer within their online invoice<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with newly created Attachment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

const body = new FileWrapper(fs.createReadStream('dummy_file'));

const includeOnline = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    invoiceID,
    fileName,
    body,
    includeOnline
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json

    {
      "AttachmentID": "5a500c1a-5a02-48de-939e-1d234fd170d4",
```

# Email Invoice

```ts
async emailInvoice(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  invoiceID: string,
  body: RequestEmpty,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<void>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `body` | [`RequestEmpty`](../../doc/models/request-empty.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**204**: Success - return response 204 no content

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance.

## Example Usage

```ts

const invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: RequestEmpty = {
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.emailInvoice(
    xeroTenantId,
    invoiceID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |

# Create Invoice History

```ts
async createInvoiceHistory(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  invoiceID: string,
  body: HistoryRecords,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<HistoryRecords>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

  historyRecords: [
    {
      details: 'Hello World',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createInvoiceHistory(
    xeroTenantId,
    invoiceID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Items

```ts
async getItems(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Items>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Items array with all Item

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'IsSold==true';

const order = 'Code ASC';

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getItems(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "8487e8d7-5fb3-4f02-b949-dec8f1e38182",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552331874897)/",
  "Items": [
    {
      "ItemID": "c8c54d65-f3f2-452d-926e-bf450b12fb07",
      "Code": "123",
      "Description": "Guitars Fender Strat",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1551981476267+0000)/",
      "PurchaseDetails": {},
      "SalesDetails": {
        "UnitPrice": 5000.0,

      },
```

# Update or Create Items

```ts
async updateOrCreateItems(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Items,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Items>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Items array with newly created Item

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: Items = {
  items: [
    {
      code: 'ItemCode123',
      description: 'Item Description ABC',
      name: 'ItemName XYZ',
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreateItems(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json

      "ItemID": "a4544d51-48f6-441f-a623-99ecbced6ab7",
```

```json
      "TotalCostPool": 25000.0,
      "QuantityOnHand": 10.0,
      "IsSold": true,
      "IsPurchased": true,
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```


# Update Item

```ts
async updateItem(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  itemID: string,
  body: Items,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Items>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `itemID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Item |
| `body` | [`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Items array with updated Item

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const itemID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: Items = {
  items: [
    {
      code: 'ItemCode123',
      description: 'Description 123',
    }
  ],
};

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateItem(
    xeroTenantId,
    itemID,
    body,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "24feb629-6b14-499e-9aa1-fc2c596c0280",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552332558975)/",
  "Items": [
    {
      "ItemID": "a7e87086-e0ae-4df2-83d7-e26e9a6b7786",
      "Code": "abc38306",
      "Description": "Hello Xero",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552332558924)/",
      "PurchaseDetails": {},
      "SalesDetails": {},
      "Name": "Hello8746",
      "IsTrackedAsInventory": false,
      "IsSold": true,
      "IsPurchased": true,
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |

# Get Journals

```ts
async getJournals(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  offset?: number,
  paymentsOnly?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Journals>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `offset` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Offset by a specified journal number. e.g. journals with a JournalNumber greater than the offset will be returned |
| `paymentsOnly` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter to retrieve journals on a cash basis. Journals are returned on an accrual basis by default. |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.journals.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Journals array with all Journals

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Journals`](../../doc/models/journals.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const offset = 10;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getJournals(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    offset
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Get Linked Transactions

```ts
async getLinkedTransactions(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  page?: number,
  linkedTransactionID?: string,
  sourceTransactionID?: string,
  contactID?: string,
  status?: string,
  targetTransactionID?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<LinkedTransactions>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Up to 100 linked transactions will be returned in a single API call. Use the page parameter to specify the page to be returned e.g. page=1. |
| `linkedTransactionID` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The Xero identifier for an Linked Transaction |
| `sourceTransactionID` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by the SourceTransactionID. Get the linked transactions created from a particular ACCPAY invoice |
| `contactID` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by the ContactID. Get all the linked transactions that have been assigned to a particular customer. |
| `status` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by the combination of ContactID and Status. Get  the linked transactions associated to a  customer and with a status |
| `targetTransactionID` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by the TargetTransactionID. Get all the linked transactions allocated to a particular ACCREC invoice |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type LinkedTransactions array with all LinkedTransaction

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`LinkedTransactions`](../../doc/models/linked-transactions.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const page = 1;

const linkedTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const sourceTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const status = 'APPROVED';

const targetTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getLinkedTransactions(
    xeroTenantId,
    page,
    linkedTransactionID,
    sourceTransactionID,
    contactID,
    status,
    targetTransactionID
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "516aabd0-e670-48d5-b0eb-10dce4494dd8",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552348338096)/",
  "LinkedTransactions": [
    {
      "LinkedTransactionID": "5cf7d9c0-b9a7-4433-a2dc-ae3c11bba39b",
      "SourceTransactionID": "aec416dd-38ea-40dc-9f0b-813c8c71f87f",
      "SourceLineItemID": "77e0b23b-5b79-4f4b-ae20-c9031d41442f",
      "ContactID": "430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8",
      "TargetTransactionID": "83693fc1-5b05-4807-b190-109d4a85dd5f",
      "TargetLineItemID": "d5128ff1-0f39-4d2a-a6d5-46dfaf5f075c",
      "Status": "ONDRAFT",
      "Type": "BILLABLEEXPENSE",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552347991000+0000)/",
      "SourceTransactionTypeCode": "ACCPAY"
    }
  ]
}
```


# Create Linked Transaction

```ts
async createLinkedTransaction(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: LinkedTransaction,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<LinkedTransactions>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`LinkedTransaction`](../../doc/models/linked-transaction.md) | Body, Required | LinkedTransaction object in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type LinkedTransactions array with newly created LinkedTransaction

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`LinkedTransactions`](../../doc/models/linked-transactions.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: LinkedTransaction = {
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createLinkedTransaction(
    xeroTenantId,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "f32b30e5-32d1-42a8-bcc9-5b22828f725c",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552351054646)/",
  "LinkedTransactions": [
    {
      "LinkedTransactionID": "e9684b6c-4df9-45a0-917b-85cc29857008",
      "SourceTransactionID": "a848644a-f20f-4630-98c3-386bd7505631",
      "SourceLineItemID": "b0df260d-3cc8-4ced-9bd6-41924f624ed3",
      "Status": "DRAFT",
      "Type": "BILLABLEEXPENSE",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552351055000+0000)/",
      "SourceTransactionTypeCode": "ACCPAY",
      "ValidationErrors": [
        {
          "Message": "The SourceLineItemID and SourceTransactionID do not match"
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |

# Update Linked Transaction

```ts
async updateLinkedTransaction(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  linkedTransactionID: string,
  body: LinkedTransactions,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<LinkedTransactions>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `linkedTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a LinkedTransaction |
| `body` | [`LinkedTransactions`](../../doc/models/linked-transactions.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type LinkedTransactions array with updated LinkedTransaction

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`LinkedTransactions`](../../doc/models/linked-transactions.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const linkedTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: LinkedTransactions = {
  linkedTransactions: [
    {
      sourceLineItemID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      sourceTransactionID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateLinkedTransaction(
    xeroTenantId,
    linkedTransactionID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Manual Journals

```ts
async getManualJournals(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  page?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ManualJournals>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 manual journals will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each overpayment |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ManualJournals array with a all ManualJournals

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="DRAFT"';

const order = 'Date ASC';

const page = 1;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getManualJournals(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    page
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*


# Update or Create Manual Journals

```ts
async updateOrCreateManualJournals(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: ManualJournals,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ManualJournals>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md) | Body, Required | ManualJournals array with ManualJournal object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ManualJournals array with newly created ManualJournal

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: ManualJournals = {
  manualJournals: [
    {
      narration: 'Journal Desc',
      date: '2019-03-14',
      journalLines: [
        {
          accountCode: '400',
          description: 'Money Movement',
          lineAmount: 100,
        },
        {
          accountCode: '400',
          description: 'Prepayment of things',
          lineAmount: -100,
          tracking: [
            {
              name: 'North',
              option: 'Region',
            }
          ],
        }
      ],
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreateManualJournals(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "45dfa608-0fcb-4f30-a377-c82cd348569c",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",

  "ManualJournals": [
    {
      "Date": "/Date(1552521600000+0000)/",
      "Status": "DRAFT",

      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552595972920+0000)/",
```

# Update Manual Journal

```ts
async updateManualJournal(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  manualJournalID: string,
  body: ManualJournals,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ManualJournals>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `manualJournalID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a ManualJournal |
| `body` | [`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ManualJournals array with an updated ManualJournal

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const manualJournalID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: ManualJournals = {
  manualJournals: [
    {
      narration: 'Hello Xero',
      journalLines: [],
      manualJournalID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateManualJournal(
    xeroTenantId,
    manualJournalID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Manual Journal Attachment by Id

```ts
async getManualJournalAttachmentById(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  manualJournalID: string,
  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `manualJournalID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a ManualJournal |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Manual Journal as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts

const manualJournalID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const contentType = 'image/jpg';

  const response = await accountingController.getManualJournalAttachmentById(
    xeroTenantId,
    manualJournalID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

```ts
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.

    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
```

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `manualJournalID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a manual journal |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const manualJournalID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: HistoryRecords = {
  historyRecords: [
    {
      details: 'Hello World',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createManualJournalHistoryRecord(
    xeroTenantId,
    manualJournalID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |

# Get Overpayments

```ts
async getOverpayments(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  page?: number,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Overpayments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 overpayments will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each overpayment |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Overpayments array with all Overpayments

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Overpayments`](../../doc/models/overpayments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

const order = 'Status ASC';

const page = 1;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getOverpayments(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    page,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Create Overpayment Allocations

```ts
async createOverpaymentAllocations(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  overpaymentID: string,
  body: Allocations,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Allocations>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `overpaymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Overpayment |
| `body` | [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md) | Body, Required | Allocations array with Allocation object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Allocations array with all Allocation for Overpayments

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const overpaymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: Allocations = {
  allocations: [
    {
      amount: 10,
      date: '2019-03-12',
      invoice: {
        contact: {
        },
        invoiceID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
        lineItems: [],
        type: Type3Enum.ACCPAY,
      },
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createOverpaymentAllocations(
    xeroTenantId,
    overpaymentID,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "3b7f7be2-384a-4703-bcfb-c56e9116c914",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
```

# Get Payments

```ts
async getPayments(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  page?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Payments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Up to 100 payments will be returned in a single API call |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Payments array for all Payments

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Payments`](../../doc/models/payments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

const order = 'Amount ASC';

const page = 1;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getPayments(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    page
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

```json
          "Message": "Payment amount exceeds the amount outstanding on this document"
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |


# Create Payments

```ts
async createPayments(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Payments,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Payments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Payments`](../../doc/models/payments.md) | Body, Required | Payments array with Payment object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Payments array for newly created Payment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Payments`](../../doc/models/payments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: Payments = {
  payments: [
    {
      account: {
        code: '970',
      },
      amount: 1,
      date: '2019-03-12',
      invoice: {
        invoiceID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
        lineItems: [],
      },
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createPayments(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Delete Payment

```ts
async deletePayment(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  paymentID: string,
  body: PaymentDelete,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Payments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `paymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Payment |
| `body` | [`PaymentDelete`](../../doc/models/payment-delete.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Payments array for updated Payment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Payments`](../../doc/models/payments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const paymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

  status: 'DELETED',
};

  const response = await accountingController.deletePayment(
    xeroTenantId,
    paymentID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);

  }
}
```

# Get Prepayments

```ts
async getPrepayments(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  page?: number,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Prepayments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 prepayments will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each overpayment |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Prepayments array for all Prepayment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Prepayments`](../../doc/models/prepayments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

const order = 'Reference ASC';

const page = 1;

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getPrepayments(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    page,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*


# Get Prepayment

```ts
async getPrepayment(
```

`accounting.transactions.read`
