# Create Prepayment Allocations

```ts
async createPrepaymentAllocations(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  prepaymentID: string,
  body: Allocations,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Allocations>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `prepaymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Prepayment |
| `body` | [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md) | Body, Required | Allocations with an array of Allocation object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Allocations array of Allocation for all Prepayment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const prepaymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: Allocations = {
  allocations: [
    {
      amount: 1,
      date: '2019-01-10',
      invoice: {
        invoiceID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
        lineItems: [],
      },
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createPrepaymentAllocations(
    xeroTenantId,
    prepaymentID,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d4758808-d14d-45d5-851a-52787ae5739a",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552522424927)/",
  "Allocations": [
    {
      "Amount": 1.0,
      "Date": "/Date(1552435200000+0000)/",
      "Invoice": {

        "Payments": [],
        "CreditNotes": [],
```

|  --- | --- | --- |

# Get Purchase Orders

```ts
async getPurchaseOrders(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  status?: Status20Enum,
  dateFrom?: string,
  dateTo?: string,
  order?: string,
  page?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<PurchaseOrders>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `status` | [`Status20Enum \| undefined`](../../doc/models/status-20-enum.md) | Query, Optional | Filter by purchase order status |
| `dateFrom` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by purchase order date (e.g. GET https://.../PurchaseOrders?DateFrom=2015-12-01&DateTo=2015-12-31 |
| `dateTo` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by purchase order date (e.g. GET https://.../PurchaseOrders?DateFrom=2015-12-01&DateTo=2015-12-31 |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | To specify a page, append the page parameter to the URL e.g. ?page=1. If there are 100 records in the response you will need to check if there is any more data by fetching the next page e.g ?page=2 and continuing this process until no more results are returned. |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type PurchaseOrder array of all PurchaseOrder

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const status = Status20Enum.SUBMITTED;

const dateFrom = '2019-12-01';

const dateTo = '2019-12-31';

const order = 'PurchaseOrderNumber ASC';

const page = 1;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getPurchaseOrders(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    status,
    dateFrom,
    dateTo,
    order,
    page
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update or Create Purchase Orders

```ts
async updateOrCreatePurchaseOrders(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: PurchaseOrders,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<PurchaseOrders>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type PurchaseOrder array for specified PurchaseOrder

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: PurchaseOrders = {
  purchaseOrders: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      },
      date: '2019-03-13',
      lineItems: [
        {
          accountCode: '710',
          description: 'Foobar',
          quantity: 1,
          unitAmount: 20,
        }
      ],
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreatePurchaseOrders(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |


# Create Purchase Orders

```ts
async createPurchaseOrders(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: PurchaseOrders,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<PurchaseOrders>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md) | Body, Required | PurchaseOrders with an array of PurchaseOrder object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type PurchaseOrder array for specified PurchaseOrder

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: PurchaseOrders = {
  purchaseOrders: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      },
      date: '2019-03-13',
      lineItems: [
        {
          accountCode: '710',
          description: 'Foobar',
          quantity: 1,
          unitAmount: 20,
        }
      ],
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createPurchaseOrders(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |

# Get Purchase Order Attachment by Id

```ts
async getPurchaseOrderAttachmentById(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  purchaseOrderID: string,
  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |

| `purchaseOrderID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Purchase Order object |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Attachment object |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Account as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts

const purchaseOrderID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

  const response = await accountingController.getPurchaseOrderAttachmentById(
    xeroTenantId,
    purchaseOrderID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `purchaseOrderID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a PurchaseOrder |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const purchaseOrderID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: HistoryRecords = {
  historyRecords: [
    {
      details: 'Hello World',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createPurchaseOrderHistory(
    xeroTenantId,
    purchaseOrderID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

# Get Quotes

```ts
async getQuotes(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  dateFrom?: string,
  dateTo?: string,
  expiryDateFrom?: string,
  expiryDateTo?: string,
  contactID?: string,
  status?: string,
  page?: number,
  order?: string,
  quoteNumber?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Quotes>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `dateFrom` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes after a particular date |
| `dateTo` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes before a particular date |
| `expiryDateFrom` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes expiring after a particular date |
| `expiryDateTo` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes before a particular date |
| `contactID` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes belonging to a particular contact |
| `status` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes of a particular Status |
| `page` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 Quotes will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each quote |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `quoteNumber` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by quote number (e.g. GET https://.../Quotes?QuoteNumber=QU-0001) |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type quotes array with all quotes

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Quotes`](../../doc/models/quotes.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const status = 'DRAFT';

const page = 1;

const order = 'Status ASC';

const quoteNumber = 'QU-0001';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getQuotes(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    undefined,
    undefined,
    undefined,
    undefined,
    contactID,
    status,
    page,
    order,
    quoteNumber
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
```

# Update or Create Quotes

```ts
async updateOrCreateQuotes(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Quotes,
  summarizeErrors?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Quotes>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Quotes`](../../doc/models/quotes.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Quotes array with updated or created Quote

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Quotes`](../../doc/models/quotes.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const body: Quotes = {
  quotes: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      },
      date: '2020-02-01',
      lineItems: [
        {
          accountCode: '12775',
          description: 'Foobar',
          quantity: 1,
          unitAmount: 20,
        }
      ],
    }
  ],
};

const summarizeErrors = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateOrCreateQuotes(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    summarizeErrors
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const quoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: Quotes = {
  quotes: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      },
      date: '2020-02-01',
      reference: 'I am an update',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateQuote(
    xeroTenantId,
    quoteID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Quote Attachments

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

```ts
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Get Quote Attachment by Id

```ts
async getQuoteAttachmentById(

  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
```

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |

| `quoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Quote object |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Attachment object |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Quote as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts

    xeroTenantId,
    quoteID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update Quote Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateQuoteAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,

  fileName: string,
  body: FileWrapper,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions

```

## Authentication

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `quoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Quote object |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the attachment |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array of Attachment

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

```ts
  const response = await accountingController.updateQuoteAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    quoteID,
    fileName,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Receipts

```ts
async getReceipts(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  ifModifiedSince?: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Receipts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `string \| undefined` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Receipts array for all Receipt

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const ifModifiedSince = '02/06/2020 20:17:43';

const where = 'Status=="DRAFT"';

const order = 'ReceiptNumber ASC';

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReceipts(
    xeroTenantId,
    ifModifiedSince,
    where,
    order,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Create Receipt

```ts
async createReceipt(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Receipts,
  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Receipts>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md) | Body, Required | Receipts with an array of Receipt object in body of request |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Receipts array for newly created Receipt

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: Receipts = {
  receipts: [
    {
      contact: {
        contactID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      },
      lineAmountTypes: LineAmountTypesEnum.NoTax,
      status: Status11Enum.DRAFT,
      user: {
        userID: '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
      },
    }
  ],
};

const unitdp = 4;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createReceipt(
    xeroTenantId,
    body,
    unitdp
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Receipt

| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

# Update Receipt

```ts
async updateReceipt(
  xeroTenantId: string,

  unitdp?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions

```

| `body` | [`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `unitdp` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

# Get Receipt Attachment by Id

```ts
async getReceiptAttachmentById(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  receiptID: string,
  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Receipt as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const contentType = 'image/jpg';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReceiptAttachmentById(
    xeroTenantId,
    receiptID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```


# Get Receipt Attachment by File Name

```ts
async getReceiptAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  receiptID: string,
  fileName: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached to the Receipt |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Receipt as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

const contentType = 'image/jpg';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReceiptAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    receiptID,
    fileName,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```


# Update Receipt Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateReceiptAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  receiptID: string,
  fileName: string,
  body: FileWrapper,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached to the Receipt |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with updated Attachment for a specified Receipt

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

const body = new FileWrapper(fs.createReadStream('dummy_file'));

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateReceiptAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    receiptID,
    fileName,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json

      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
```

# Create Receipt History

```ts
async createReceiptHistory(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  receiptID: string,
  body: HistoryRecords,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<HistoryRecords>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

  historyRecords: [
    {
      details: 'Hello World',
    }
  ],
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.createReceiptHistory(
    xeroTenantId,
    receiptID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Repeating Invoice Attachment by Id

```ts
async getRepeatingInvoiceAttachmentById(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  repeatingInvoiceID: string,
  attachmentID: string,
  contentType: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `repeatingInvoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Repeating Invoice |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Repeating Invoice as binary data

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type `NodeJS.ReadableStream | Blob`.

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const repeatingInvoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const contentType = 'image/jpg';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getRepeatingInvoiceAttachmentById(
    xeroTenantId,
    repeatingInvoiceID,
    attachmentID,
    contentType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Update Repeating Invoice Attachment by File Name

```ts
async updateRepeatingInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  repeatingInvoiceID: string,
  fileName: string,
  body: FileWrapper,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Attachments>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `repeatingInvoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Repeating Invoice |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached to a Repeating Invoice |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with specified Attachment for a specified Repeating Invoice

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const repeatingInvoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

const body = new FileWrapper(fs.createReadStream('dummy_file'));

try {
  const response = await accountingController.updateRepeatingInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
    xeroTenantId,
    repeatingInvoiceID,
    fileName,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "61b24d5c-4d6e-468f-9de1-abbc234b239a",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1553805873362)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "d086d5f4-9c3d-4edc-a87e-906248eeb652",
      "FileName": "HelloWorld.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/RepeatingInvoices/428c0d75-909f-4b04-8403-a48dc27283b0/Attachments/HelloWorld.jpg",
      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
}
```

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`CustomError`](../../doc/models/custom-error.md) |

# Get Report Aged Receivables by Contact

```ts
async getReportAgedReceivablesByContact(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  contactId: string,
  date?: string,
  fromDate?: string,
  toDate?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ReportWithRows>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactId` | `string` | Query, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `date` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The date of the Aged Receivables By Contact report |
| `fromDate` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The from date of the Aged Receivables By Contact report |
| `toDate` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The to date of the Aged Receivables By Contact report |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const contactId = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReportAgedReceivablesByContact(
    xeroTenantId,
    contactId
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Get Report Balance Sheet

```ts
async getReportBalanceSheet(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  date?: string,
  periods?: number,
  timeframe?: TimeframeEnum,
  trackingOptionID1?: string,
  trackingOptionID2?: string,
  standardLayout?: boolean,
  paymentsOnly?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ReportWithRows>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `date` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The date of the Balance Sheet report |
| `periods` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The number of periods for the Balance Sheet report |
| `timeframe` | [`TimeframeEnum \| undefined`](../../doc/models/timeframe-enum.md) | Query, Optional | The period size to compare to (MONTH, QUARTER, YEAR) |
| `trackingOptionID1` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The tracking option 1 for the Balance Sheet report |
| `trackingOptionID2` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The tracking option 2 for the Balance Sheet report |
| `standardLayout` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The standard layout boolean for the Balance Sheet report |
| `paymentsOnly` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | return a cash basis for the Balance Sheet report |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const date = '2019-11-01';

const periods = 3;

const timeframe = TimeframeEnum.MONTH;

const trackingOptionID1 = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const trackingOptionID2 = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const standardLayout = true;

const paymentsOnly = false;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReportBalanceSheet(
    xeroTenantId,
    date,
    periods,
    timeframe,
    trackingOptionID1,
    trackingOptionID2,
    standardLayout,
    paymentsOnly
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Get Report Bank Summary

```ts
async getReportBankSummary(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  fromDate?: string,
  toDate?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ReportWithRows>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `fromDate` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The from date for the Bank Summary report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `toDate` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The to date for the Bank Summary report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const fromDate = '2019-11-01';

const toDate = '2019-11-30';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReportBankSummary(
    xeroTenantId,
    fromDate,
    toDate
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
```

# Get Report Budget Summary

```ts
async getReportBudgetSummary(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  date?: string,
  period?: number,
  timeframe?: number,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ReportWithRows>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `date` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The date for the Bank Summary report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `period` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The number of periods to compare (integer between 1 and 12) |
| `timeframe` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The period size to compare to (1=month, 3=quarter, 12=year) |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: success- return a Report with Rows object

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const date = '2019-03-31';

const period = 2;

const timeframe = 3;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReportBudgetSummary(
    xeroTenantId,
    date,
    period,
    timeframe
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Get Report Profit and Loss

```ts
async getReportProfitAndLoss(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  fromDate?: string,
  toDate?: string,
  periods?: number,
  timeframe?: TimeframeEnum,
  trackingCategoryID?: string,
  trackingCategoryID2?: string,
  trackingOptionID?: string,
  trackingOptionID2?: string,
  standardLayout?: boolean,
  paymentsOnly?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ReportWithRows>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `fromDate` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The from date for the ProfitAndLoss report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `toDate` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The to date for the ProfitAndLoss report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `periods` | `number \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The number of periods to compare (integer between 1 and 12) |
| `timeframe` | [`TimeframeEnum \| undefined`](../../doc/models/timeframe-enum.md) | Query, Optional | The period size to compare to (MONTH, QUARTER, YEAR) |
| `trackingCategoryID` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The trackingCategory 1 for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `trackingCategoryID2` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The trackingCategory 2 for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `trackingOptionID` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The tracking option 1 for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `trackingOptionID2` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The tracking option 2 for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `standardLayout` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Return the standard layout for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `paymentsOnly` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Return cash only basis for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const fromDate = '2019-03-01';

const toDate = '2019-03-31';

const periods = 3;

const timeframe = TimeframeEnum.MONTH;

const trackingCategoryID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const trackingCategoryID2 = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const trackingOptionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const trackingOptionID2 = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const standardLayout = true;

const paymentsOnly = false;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReportProfitAndLoss(
    xeroTenantId,
    fromDate,
    toDate,
    periods,
    timeframe,
    trackingCategoryID,
    trackingCategoryID2,
    trackingOptionID,
    trackingOptionID2,
    standardLayout,
    paymentsOnly
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```


# Get Report Ten Ninety Nine

```ts
async getReportTenNinetyNine(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  reportYear?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<Reports>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `reportYear` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The year of the 1099 report |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.tenninetynine.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Reports

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`Reports`](../../doc/models/reports.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const reportYear = '2019';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReportTenNinetyNine(
    xeroTenantId,
    reportYear
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Get Report Trial Balance

```ts
async getReportTrialBalance(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  date?: string,
  paymentsOnly?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ReportWithRows>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `date` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | The date for the Trial Balance report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `paymentsOnly` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Return cash only basis for the Trial Balance report |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const date = '2019-10-31';

const paymentsOnly = true;

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReportTrialBalance(
    xeroTenantId,
    date,
    paymentsOnly
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

# Get Report BA Sor GST

```ts
async getReportBASorGST(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  reportID: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ReportWithRows>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `reportID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Report |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const reportID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getReportBASorGST(
    xeroTenantId,
    reportID
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```


# Post Setup

```ts
async postSetup(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  body: Setup,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<ImportSummaryObject>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Setup`](../../doc/models/setup.md) | Body, Required | Object including an accounts array, a conversion balances array and a conversion date object in body of request |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - returns a summary of the chart of accounts updates

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`ImportSummaryObject`](../../doc/models/import-summary-object.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const body: Setup = {
  accounts: [
    {
      code: '200',
      name: 'Sales',
      reportingCode: 'REV.TRA.GOO',
      type: AccountTypeEnum.SALES,
    },
    {
      code: '400',
      name: 'Advertising',
      reportingCode: 'EXP',
      type: AccountTypeEnum.OVERHEADS,
    },
    {
      code: '610',
      name: 'Accounts Receivable',
      reportingCode: 'ASS.CUR.REC.TRA',
      type: AccountTypeEnum.CURRENT,
    },
    {
      code: '800',
      name: 'Accounts Payable',
      reportingCode: 'LIA.CUR.PAY',
      type: AccountTypeEnum.CURRLIAB,
    }
  ],
  conversionBalances: [],
  conversionDate: {
  },
};

try {
  const response = await accountingController.postSetup(
    xeroTenantId,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "80dcb65b-4d14-4350-84e6-1438a809244a",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Java Public Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1604457589645)/",
  "ImportSummary": {
    "Accounts": {
      "Total": 17,
      "New": 0,
      "Updated": 8,
      "Deleted": 0,
      "Locked": 0,
      "System": 9,
      "Errored": 0,
      "Present": true,
      "NewOrUpdated": 8
    },
    "Organisation": {
      "Present": false
    }
  }
}
```


# Get Tax Rates

```ts
async getTaxRates(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  taxType?: string,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<TaxRates>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `taxType` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by tax type |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type TaxRates array with TaxRates

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`TaxRates`](../../doc/models/tax-rates.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const where = 'Status=="ACTIVE"';

const order = 'Name ASC';

const taxType = 'INPUT';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.getTaxRates(
    xeroTenantId,
    where,
    order,
    taxType
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
```

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`TaxRates`](../../doc/models/tax-rates.md).

```ts
      status: Status19Enum.DELETED,
      taxComponents: [
        {
          name: 'State Tax',
          rate: 2.25,
        }
      ],
    }
  ],
};

    xeroTenantId,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Get Tracking Categories

```ts
async getTrackingCategories(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  where?: string,
  order?: string,
  includeArchived?: boolean,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<TrackingCategories>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `where` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `string \| undefined` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `includeArchived` | `boolean \| undefined` | Query, Optional | e.g. includeArchived=true - Categories and options with a status of ARCHIVED will be included in the response |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type TrackingCategories array of TrackingCategory

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`TrackingCategories`](../../doc/models/tracking-categories.md).

## Example Usage

```ts

const order = 'Name ASC';

  const response = await accountingController.getTrackingCategories(
    xeroTenantId,
    where,
    order
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
  }
}
```


**200**: Success - return response of type TrackingOptions array of remaining options for a specified category

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`TrackingOptions`](../../doc/models/tracking-options.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const trackingCategoryID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const trackingOptionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

try {
  const response = await accountingController.deleteTrackingOptions(
    xeroTenantId,
    trackingCategoryID,
    trackingOptionID
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```

# Update Tracking Options

```ts
async updateTrackingOptions(
  xeroTenantId: string,
  trackingCategoryID: string,
  trackingOptionID: string,
  body: TrackingOption,
  requestOptions?: RequestOptions
): Promise<ApiResponse<TrackingOptions>>
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `trackingCategoryID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a TrackingCategory |
| `trackingOptionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Tracking Option |
| `body` | [`TrackingOption`](../../doc/models/tracking-option.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `requestOptions` | `RequestOptions \| undefined` | Optional | Pass additional request options. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type TrackingOptions array of options for a specified category

This method returns an [`ApiResponse`](../../doc/api-response.md) instance. The `result` property of this instance returns the response data which is of type [`TrackingOptions`](../../doc/models/tracking-options.md).

## Example Usage

```ts
const xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

const trackingCategoryID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const trackingOptionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

const body: TrackingOption = {
};

  const response = await accountingController.updateTrackingOptions(
    xeroTenantId,
    trackingCategoryID,
    trackingOptionID,
    body
  );

  // Extracting fully parsed response body.
  console.log(response.result);

  // Extracting response status code.
  console.log(response.statusCode);
  // Extracting response headers.
  console.log(response.headers);
  // Extracting response body of type `string | Stream`
  console.log(response.body);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ApiError) {
    // Extracting response error status code.
    console.log(error.statusCode);
    // Extracting response error headers.
    console.log(error.headers);
    // Extracting response error body of type `string | Stream`.
    console.log(error.body);
    if (error instanceof CustomError) {
      console.log(error.result);
    }
  }
}
```
